# Data Administration - UI Design Specification

## ğŸ“‹ Executive Summary

The Data Administration module provides admin-level configuration capabilities for managing checklist types, checklist templates, email templates, AI prompts, and reference data (geography, job titles, businesses). This is the central hub for customizing the HRMS system behavior.

**Pages:**
- Checklist Type Management: `/hrms/admin/checklist-types`
- Checklist Templates: `/hrms/admin/checklist-templates`
- Email Templates: `/hrms/admin/email-templates`
- AI Prompts (Newsletter): `/hrms/admin/ai-prompts`
- Businesses: `/hrms/admin/businesses` (CRM Linked)
- Countries: `/hrms/admin/countries` (CRM Linked)
- States: `/hrms/admin/states` (CRM Linked)
- Cities: `/hrms/admin/cities` (CRM Linked)
- IT Job Titles: `/hrms/admin/job-titles` (CRM Linked)
- LCA Job Titles: `/hrms/admin/lca-job-titles` (HRMS Only)
- Visa Status: `/hrms/admin/visa-status` (CRM Linked)
- Resend API Keys: `/hrms/admin/resend-api-keys` (CRM Linked)
- Invite Users: `/hrms/admin/invite-users` (CRM Linked)
- User Role Assignments: `/hrms/admin/user-roles` (CRM Linked)
- Access Control: `/hrms/admin/access-control` (CRM Linked)

**Access Level:** HRMS Admin only  
**Primary Function:** System configuration, user management, and template management

**Security Requirements:**
- `/hrms/admin/*` access is restricted by RBAC and must be enforced server-side (Edge Functions/DB), not only by hiding UI.
- Admin access requires MFA enabled.
- Sensitive admin actions (user roles/access control, invite users, API keys/integration secrets) require â€œrecent authenticationâ€.
- All admin data access remains tenant-isolated via RLS.

See [UI_DESIGN_DOCS/19_AUTHENTICATION_AUTHORIZATION_SECURITY.md](19_AUTHENTICATION_AUTHORIZATION_SECURITY.md).

---

### 12.3 CRM Table Reference

**Table:** `business_email_settings` (from CRM)

| Column | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `setting_id` | UUID | Primary key |
| `tenant_id` | UUID | Tenant reference |
| `business_id` | UUID | Business reference |
| `resend_api_key` | TEXT | Encrypted API key |
| `from_email` | VARCHAR(255) | Sender email address |
| `from_name` | VARCHAR(255) | Sender display name |
| `reply_to_email` | VARCHAR(255) | Reply-to address |
| `is_verified` | BOOLEAN | Verification status |
| `last_verified_at` | TIMESTAMPTZ | Last verification time |

---

## ğŸ‘¤ 13. Invite Users (CRM Linked)

### 13.3 CRM Tables Reference

**Table:** `user_invitations` (from CRM)

| Column | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `invitation_id` | UUID | Primary key |
| `tenant_id` | UUID | Tenant reference |
| `email` | VARCHAR(255) | Invitee email |
| `first_name` | VARCHAR(100) | First name |
| `last_name` | VARCHAR(100) | Last name |
| `role_id` | UUID | Assigned role |
| `invited_by` | UUID | Inviter user ID |
| `invitation_token` | TEXT | Unique token |
| `expires_at` | TIMESTAMPTZ | Expiration time |
| `accepted_at` | TIMESTAMPTZ | Acceptance time |
| `status` | VARCHAR(50) | pending/accepted/expired/revoked |

---

## ğŸ” 14. User Role Assignments (CRM Linked)

### 14.3 CRM Tables Reference

**Table:** `user_role_assignments` (from CRM)

| Column | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `assignment_id` | UUID | Primary key |
| `user_id` | UUID | User reference |
| `tenant_id` | UUID | Tenant reference |
| `role_id` | UUID | Role reference |
| `assigned_by` | UUID | Admin who assigned |
| `assigned_at` | TIMESTAMPTZ | Assignment time |

**Table:** `roles` (from CRM)

| Column | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `role_id` | UUID | Primary key |
| `tenant_id` | UUID | Tenant reference |
| `role_name` | VARCHAR(100) | Role display name |
| `role_code` | VARCHAR(50) | Role identifier |
| `role_level` | INTEGER | Permission level (1-10) |
| `description` | TEXT | Role description |
| `is_system_role` | BOOLEAN | Cannot be deleted |

---

### 15.3 CRM Tables Reference

**Table:** `role_permissions` (from CRM)

| Column | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `permission_id` | UUID | Primary key |
| `role_id` | UUID | Role reference |
| `module_code` | VARCHAR(100) | Module identifier |
| `permission_code` | VARCHAR(100) | Permission identifier |
| `can_view` | BOOLEAN | View permission |
| `can_create` | BOOLEAN | Create permission |
| `can_edit` | BOOLEAN | Edit permission |
| `can_delete` | BOOLEAN | Delete permission |

**Table:** `modules` (from CRM)

| Column | Type | Description |
|--------|------|-------------|
| `module_id` | UUID | Primary key |
| `module_code` | VARCHAR(100) | Module identifier |
| `module_name` | VARCHAR(255) | Display name |
| `parent_module_id` | UUID | Parent module (hierarchy) |
| `display_order` | INTEGER | Sort order |
| `is_hrms_module` | BOOLEAN | HRMS-specific module |

---

## âœ… 16. Validation Rules

### Checklist Type Validations

| Field | Validation | Error Message |
|-------|------------|---------------|
| Type Code | Required, unique, lowercase + underscores only | "Type code must be unique and contain only lowercase letters and underscores" |
| Type Name | Required, 3-255 chars | "Type name is required (3-255 characters)" |
| Target Table | Required, must exist in database | "Selected table does not exist" |
| Target ID Column | Required, must exist in selected table | "Selected column does not exist in table" |

### Checklist Template Validations

| Field | Validation | Error Message |
|-------|------------|---------------|
| Template Name | Required, 3-255 chars | "Template name is required" |
| Checklist Type | Required | "Please select a checklist type" |
| Employee Type | Required if checklist type requires it | "Employee type is required for this checklist type" |
| At least one group | Required | "Template must have at least one group" |

### Email Template Validations

| Field | Validation | Error Message |
|-------|------------|---------------|
| Template Name | Required, 3-255 chars | "Template name is required" |
| Template Key | Required, unique, lowercase + underscores | "Template key must be unique" |
| Subject | Required, max 500 chars | "Subject line is required" |
| Body HTML | Required | "Email body is required" |
| Variables | Must be valid syntax | "Invalid variable syntax: {{variable_name}}" |

### AI Prompt Validations

| Field | Validation | Error Message |
|-------|------------|---------------|
| Prompt Name | Required, 3-255 chars | "Prompt name is required" |
| Prompt Key | Required, unique, lowercase + underscores | "Prompt key must be unique" |
| System Prompt | Required, min 50 chars | "System prompt is required (min 50 characters)" |
| Temperature | 0.0 - 2.0 | "Temperature must be between 0 and 2" |
| Max Tokens | 100 - 8000 | "Max tokens must be between 100 and 8000" |

### LCA Job Title Validations

| Field | Validation | Error Message |
|-------|------------|---------------|
| LCA Job Title | Required, 3-255 chars | "LCA Job Title is required" |
| SOC Code | Required, format XX-XXXX | "SOC Code must be in format XX-XXXX (e.g., 15-1252)" |
| Wage Level | Required, 1-4 | "Please select a wage level" |

### CRM-Linked Entity Validations

| Entity | Validation | Error Message |
|--------|------------|---------------|
| Business Short Name | Required, 2-10 chars, unique | "Short name must be unique and 2-10 characters" |
| Country ISO Code | Required, 2-3 chars, unique | "ISO code must be unique" |
| State Code | Required, 2-3 chars, unique per country | "State code must be unique within the country" |
| Visa Type | Required, unique | "Visa type name must be unique" |

---

## â™¿ 17. Accessibility

### Keyboard Navigation

| Key | Action |
|-----|--------|
| `Tab` | Navigate between form fields |
| `Enter` | Submit forms, expand groups |
| `Escape` | Close modals |
| `Arrow Up/Down` | Navigate dropdown options |
| `Space` | Toggle checkboxes |

### Screen Reader Support

```html
<section aria-label="Checklist template builder">
  <h2 id="template-heading">Template: IT USA Immigration Checklist</h2>
  
  <div role="group" aria-labelledby="group-1">
    <h3 id="group-1">Immigration Documents (4 items)</h3>
    <ul role="list">
      <li role="listitem">
        <span>I-9 Form</span>
        <span class="sr-only">Required item with compliance tracking enabled</span>
      </li>
    </ul>
  </div>
</section>
```

### Role Hierarchy

| Role | Level | Description |
|------|-------|-------------|
| Super Admin | 10 | Full system access |
| HRMS Admin | 8 | HRMS configuration & management |
| HR Manager | 6 | Employee & compliance management |
| Immigration Specialist | 6 | Immigration & visa management |
| HR Staff | 4 | Basic HR operations |
| Employee | 1 | Self-service only |
